add_namespace = nea
#kmt refuse, cliques consider joining
country_event = {
	id = nea.1
	title = nea.1.t
	desc = nea.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #join
		name = nea.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = event_target:scp_war_opposition_leader
			}
			country_event = { days = 3 id = nea.2 }
		}
	}
	option = { #not join
		name = nea.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TAG = PRC
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_global_flag = gud_ready
						GXC = { has_offensive_war_with = CHI }
					}
					AND = {
						OR = {
							tag = GUD
							tag = GXC
							tag = SIC
							tag = SHC
							tag = SHD
						}
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					tag = SHX
					tag = SUY
					tag = YUN
					tag = HPC
					tag = XIK
					tag = PLM
					tag = XSM
					tag = NXM
					tag = GSM
					tag = EGM
					tag = TNG
					tag = HMI
				    tag = KHR
					tag = KRS
					tag = ATM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
###join prc fight chiang###
country_event = {
	id = nea.2
	title = nea.2.t
	desc = nea.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_02
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = nea.2.a
		trigger = {
			tag = PRC
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = nea.2.b
		trigger = { is_faction_leader = yes }
		ROOT = {
			add_to_faction = FROM
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						is_subject_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					}
				}
				event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
					end_puppet = FROM
				}
			}
		}
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
			FROM = {
				add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = ROOT enemy = PREV }
			}
		}
			
	}
	option = {
		name = nea.2.c
		trigger = { TAG = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader }
	}
}
####NEW NATIONAL LEADERSHIP, triggered when a non-CHI_power_struggle warlord won against old leader
country_event = {
	id = nea.3
	title = nea.3.t
	desc = nea.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_flag
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#trigger = {
		 #used to stop multiple warlords from becoming china, in case of multiple warlords have similar war participationa against china
		
	#}
	#trigger = {
	#	#tag = NEA
	#	is_warlord = yes
	#	NOT = {
	#		tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
	#	}
	#	NOT = {
	#		has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
	#		is_subject_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
	#	}
	#	owns_state = 1015
	#	#has_country_flag = yang_hucheng_in_charge
	#}
	option = {
		name = nea.3.a
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				save_event_target_as = old_leader
				clr_country_flag = wtt_political_struggle
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader # warlord has taken over before this happened
							has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_PRC
							has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_second_republic_red
							has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_second_republic_blue
							has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_second_republic
						}
					}
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						tag = CHI
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_power_struggle_defeated
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = new_leader
			CHI_negative_spirit_transfer = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = lushan_declaration_flag
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = generallissimo
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = CHI_power_struggle_defeated
				}
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_puppet = no
							has_country_flag = cooperation_with_communist_flag
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_PRC
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							is_puppet = no
							NOT = {
								has_country_flag = CHI_opposition_flag
							}
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_warlord_leader
					}
				}
			}
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.small_china
			tooltip = small_china_tt
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1 id = nea.6 #to clear new_china_determined
			}
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				if = {	limit = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
					set_variable = { global.previous_china_leader = THIS }
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = scp_war_old_leader
			clear_global_event_target = scp_war_opposition_leader
			clear_global_event_target = WTT_current_china_leader
			clr_global_flag = wtt_war_over_national_leadership
			save_global_event_target_as = WTT_current_china_leader
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				name = CHI_democratic_party
				long_name = CHI_democratic_party_long
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				name = CHI_fascism_party
				long_name = CHI_fascism_party_long
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = n_socialism
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = n_socialism
				name = CHI_n_socialism_party
				long_name = CHI_n_socialism_party_long
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = china_government_legitimacy
			}
		}
		WTT_restart_political_struggle = yes
	}
}

		}
	}

	}

					OR = {
						has_war_with = HPC

				}
			}
		}
	}

				OR = {
					has_war_with = HPC

			has_war_with = JAP
		}

#chi offer peace
country_event = {
	id = gxc.4
	title = gxc.4.t
	desc = gxc.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chen_and_li

	#mean_time_to_happen = {
		#	days = 10
		#}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = { #peace#accept
		name = gxc.4.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LG_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = REBELLION
				}
			}
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_global_flag = buy_gud_army_fail
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = { days = 5 id = rcmchina.237 }#GXC accept peace
		}
		GUD = { country_event = { id = gxc.6 } }
		add_political_power = 50
		set_country_flag = gxc_accept_peace
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EFM_Southwest_two_agencies
			}
			remove_ideas = EFM_Southwest_two_agencies
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GXC_Japanese_consultant
			}
			remove_ideas = GXC_Japanese_consultant
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			white_peace = FROM
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GXC
				has_war_with = XIA 
			}
			white_peace = XIA
		}
		if = {
		    limit = {
			    is_in_faction = yes 
		    }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
		    limit = {
			    is_faction_leader = yes
			    NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GUD }
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
	    #set_rule = { can_create_factions = no }
	    clr_global_flag = liangguang_on_going
		clr_global_flag = gxc_join_2g
		set_global_flag = gxc_peace_liangguang
	}
	option = { #war
		name = gxc.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = LG_AI_BEHAVIOR
						option = AHISTORICAL
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_global_flag = buy_gud_army_fail }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LG_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = HISTORICAL
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LG_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = PEACE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = LG_AI_BEHAVIOR
					option = REBELLION
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 500
				has_global_flag = buy_gud_army_fail
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			country_event = { days = 5 id = rcmchina.238 }
		}
	    clr_global_flag = liangguang_on_going
	    set_global_flag = liangguang_on_gxc_rebel
	}
}

#chi war
country_event = {
	id = gxc.5
	title = gxc.5.t
	desc = gxc.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chiang_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = gxc.5.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = GXC
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = CHI
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = CHI type = annex_everything }
				else = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = CHI
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GXC
				GUD = { is_in_faction_with = GXC }
				has_global_flag = gud_ready
			}
			GUD = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GXC enemy = CHI } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GUD
				GXC = { is_in_faction_with = GUD }
				has_global_flag = gxc_ready
			}
			GXC = { add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GXC enemy = CHI } }
		}
	    if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GXC 
			}
            clr_global_flag = liangguang_on_going
		    set_global_flag = liangguang_on_gxc_rebel 
			complete_national_focus = GXC_Challenge_central_government
		} 
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gxc.14
	title = gxc.14.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_bai_bribed
	desc = {
		text = gxc.14.d_chi
		trigger = { TAG = CHI }
	}
	desc = {
		text = gxc.14.d
		trigger = { NOT = { TAG = CHI } }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = buy_gxc
	}
	option = {
		name = gxc.14.a
		trigger = { TAG = CHI }
		GXC = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_template = "Mint'uan"
				}
				set_division_template_lock = {
					division_template = "Mint'uan"
					is_locked = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_template = "Fei Chêngkuei Chün"
				}
				delete_unit_template_and_units = {
					division_template = "Fei Chêngkuei Chün"
					disband = no
				}
			}
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_id = 2505
					}
				}
				set_nationality = ROOT
			}
		}
		annex_country = { target = GXC transfer_troops = yes }
	    clr_global_flag = gxc_join_2g
	}
	option = {
		name = gxc.14.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { TAG = CHI }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GXC
			}
		    custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
			effect_tooltip = {
                if = {
					limit = {
						has_template = "Mint'uan"
					}
					set_division_template_lock = {
						division_template = "Mint'uan"
						is_locked = no
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
				}
			}	
		}

		#dismantle_faction = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = GXC
				}
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
                CHI = {
					annex_country = { target = GXC transfer_troops = yes }
				}
			}	
		    if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = XIA 
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_ally_with = ROOT
					}
					white_peace = XIA
				}
				white_peace = XIA
			}	
			XIA = {
				country_event = gxc.44 #annex 
			}
		}
	    #set_rule = { can_create_factions = no }
	}
}

							}
						}

					}

					}
				}

					limit = {
						749 = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
					}

					set_state_owner = 749
					if = {
						limit = {
							749 = {
								is_controlled_by = ROOT
							}
						}
						set_state_controller = 749
					}
					set_state_owner = 749
					749 = { 
						add_compliance = 25
						force_disable_resistance = GXC
						#add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = new_guangxi_clique_modifier scope = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader } 
						#add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = new_guangxi_clique_modifier scope = GXC }
						set_state_flag = new_guangxi_clique_flag
					}
				}

						is_mr5_state = yes

							}

					}

	desc = gxc.22.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = gxc.22.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CHI
			}
			#CHI_he_jian = {
			#	set_nationality = XIA 
			#}
			CHI_liu_jianxu = {
				set_nationality = XIA 
			}
			CHI_li_jue = {
				set_nationality = XIA 
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = XIA 
				}
				transfer_state_to = XIA 
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = XIA         # the recipient
					size = 0            # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
					army_ratio = 0       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
					#stockpile_ratio = 0.3  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
					#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
					#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
						always = yes
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					ROOT = {
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 1 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 2 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 3 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 4 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 5 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 6 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
						delete_unit = { 
							id = 7 # can be filtered to a given id in create unit effect 
							state = PREV
							disband = no # default is no. if set to yes the game will refund equipment/manpower
						}
					}
				}
				#delete_unit_template_and_units = { #remove when war breaks out
				#    division_template = "Hunan Luchün Shih"
				#    disband = no
			    #}
		        #delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				#    division_template = "Hunan T'iaocheng Shih"
				#    disband = no
			    #}
			    #delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				#    division_template = "Hunan Chengli Shih"
				#    disband = no
			    #}
			    #delete_unit_template_and_units = {
				#    division_template = "Hunan Tuli Lü"
				#    disband = no
			    #}
			    #delete_unit_template_and_units = {
			    #   division_template = "Hunan Paoan T'uan"
				#    disband = no
			    #}
				XIA = {
					add_ideas = {
						warlord_economy
						PRC_government_corruption
						CHI_fractured_administration_idea_1
						CHI_incompetent_officers
						incompetent_heavy_industry
						unbalanced_industry
						iliterate_population
						no_proper_equipment_design
						CHI_militia_idea
						GXC_hunan_idea
					}
					inherit_technology = CHI
					load_oob = XIA_1936
					load_focus_tree = { tree = china_warlord_focus keep_completed = yes }
					country_event = { id = gxc.21 days = 5 }
				} 	
			}
		}
		else = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				CHI = {
					CHI_liu_jianxu = {
						set_nationality = XIA 
					}
					CHI_li_jue = {
						set_nationality = XIA 
					}
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							is_core_of = XIA 
						}
						transfer_state_to = XIA 
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = XIA         # the recipient
						size = 0            # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
						army_ratio = 0       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
						#stockpile_ratio = 0.3  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
						#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
						#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
							always = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			XIA = { country_event = { id = gxc.21 days = 5 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #central peaces with 2G, to 2G leader
	id = gxc.27
	title = gxc.27.t
	desc = gxc.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = gxc.27.a
		#status quo ante bellum
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				FROM = { surrender_progress < 0.2 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = gxc.28 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_green
		effect_tooltip = {
			white_peace = FROM
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				white_peace = FROM
			}
		}
		
	}

	option = {
		name = gxc.27.b
		#keep all lands we got
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				FROM = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = gxc.29 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_green
		effect_tooltip = {
			white_peace = FROM
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				white_peace = FROM
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = FROM
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gxc.27.b
		#no peace!
		FROM = { country_event = gxc.31 }
		add_war_support = -0.1
	}
}

		effect_tooltip = {
			event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = XIA        # the recipient
					size = 0            # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
					army_ratio = 0.05      # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
					#stockpile_ratio = 0.3  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
					#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
					#air_ratio = 0        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air

						always = yes
					}
				}
			}	
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		activate_mission = GUD_hunan_mission
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_ai = no
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				target = XIA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
				is_ai = no
				all_allied_country = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				target = XIA
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_ai = yes
				all_allied_country = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = XIA
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = { GXC = { has_war_with = CHI } }
			add_to_war = { targeted_alliance = GXC enemy = CHI }
			GXC = {
				if = { limit = { GXC = { is_faction_leader = no } }
					set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
					create_faction = "anti_jap_salv_army"
					add_to_faction = GUD
					#GUD = { set_faction_leader = yes }
				}
				if = { limit = { GXC = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
					add_to_faction = GUD
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GXC = { NOT = { has_war_with = CHI } } }
			set_global_flag = gud_ready
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = NXM_GAN
			set_country_flag = im_gansu_ma_clique_now
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #1044 is gonna fail, retreat to ningsia?
	id = nxm.3
	title = nxm.3.t
	desc = nxm.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ma_hongkui_ousted
	is_triggered_only = yes 

	option = {
		name = nxm.3.a
		#join ningsia
		trigger = {
			NXM = {
				exists = yes
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					has_border_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		NXM = {
			country_event = nxm.4
		}
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			target = NXM       # the recipient
			size = 1           # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
			army_ratio = 1       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
			stockpile_ratio = 1  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
			navy_ratio = 1     # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
			air_ratio = 1       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
				always = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = PRC
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1029
						state = 939
						state = 1044
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PRC
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NXM_ma_hongbin = {
                remove_country_leader_role = {
					ideology = despotism
					ideology = fascism_ideology
					ideology = conservatism
					ideology = marxism
					ideology = n_socialism_ideology
				}
			}
			
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_character = NXM_ma_hongbin
					#is_character = NXM_ma_tengjiao
					is_character = NXM_ma_duijing
				}
			}
			set_nationality = NXM
		}
		#NXM = {
		#	annex_country = { target = ROOT transfer_troops = yes }
		#}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NXM = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
			NXM = {
				change_tag_from = ROOT
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nxm.3.b
		#no
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}
}

#PRC advances, reinforce Gansu
country_event = {
	id = qng.3
	title = qng.3.t
	desc = qng.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_mong_army_01
	fire_only_once = yes
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = XSM
		date < 1938.5.1
		PRC = {
			has_war_with = GSM
			#controls_province = 12327
			controls_province = 5057
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = qng.3.a
		#transfer_units_fraction = {
		#	target = GSM          # the recipient
		#	size = 0            # [0,1] Default value for the ratio below if they are not specified
		#	army_ratio = 0.15       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for army
			#stockpile_ratio = 0.3  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
			#navy_ratio = 0.2       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
			#air_ratio = 0.4        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
		#	keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
		#		always = yes
		#	}
		#}
		set_global_flag = prc_adv_1_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_manpower > 2999
			}
			add_manpower = -3000
			GSM = {
				add_manpower = 3000
			}
		}
		GSM = {
			add_offsite_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
			add_to_variable = { GSM.ammunition_variable = 6 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = give_some_ammo
		XSM = {
			add_to_variable = { ammunition_variable = -6 }
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = xik 

# Xikang Provincial Government established
country_event = {
	id = xik.1
	title = xik.1.t
	desc = xik.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_great_way
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
    immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				1042 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = { state = 751 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = xik.1.a
		add_political_power = 100
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		transfer_state = 751
		add_state_core = 751
		if = {
			limit = {
				1042 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			set_victory_points = {
				province = 2067
				value = 1
			}
			set_victory_points = {
				province = 4999
				value = 5
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = { state = 1042 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = shx.1.d

		always = no #the original thing is actually historical
		tag = SHX
		has_war = yes
		NOT = {
			controls_state = 615
		}
		controls_state = 621
	}
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 5
	#}

	}

	id = shx.3
	title = shx.3.t
	desc = shx.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_sinkiang_join_PRC
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = no
	trigger = {
		tag = SHX
		NOT = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		}
		has_war_with = JAP
		any_other_country = {
			exists = yes
			tag = SUY
			is_in_faction_with = ROOT
		}
		NOT = {
			SUY = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		date > 1940.1.1
	}
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 5
	#}
	option = {
		name = shx.3.a
		SHX_chen_changjie = {
			set_nationality = SUY
		}
		#SHX_Lu_Yinglin = {
		#	set_nationality = SUY
		#}
		SUY = {
			country_event = {
				id = shx.4 days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #pailingmiao mutiny
	id = shx.19
	title = shx.19.t
	desc = shx.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_mong_army_01
	is_triggered_only = no
	trigger = {
		#has_global_flag = de_wang_defect_flag
		tag = ECA
		has_character = PLM_prince_demchugdongrub
		num_divisions > 1
        any_neighbor_country = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				is_subject_of = JAP
				has_completed_focus = SHX_Support_north_china_buffer_state_strategy
			}
			OR = {
				tag = SUY
				tag = SHX
			}
		}
		1014 = {
			is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = pailingmiao_mutiny_flag
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = shx.19.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				SUY = {
					is_neighbor_of = ROOT
					exists = yes
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = SHX
						is_subject_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					}
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT 
					}
				}
			}
			SUY = {
				country_event = shx.20
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
                if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = PLM_zhu_shifu
					}
					PLM_zhu_shifu = {
						set_nationality = SUY
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = PLM_bai_haifeng
					}
					PLM_bai_haifeng = {
						set_nationality = SUY
					}
				}
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					target = SUY      # the recipient			                      
					size = 0 
					army_ratio = 0.01      # Overrides size modifier for army
					stockpile_ratio = 0  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
					navy_ratio = 0       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
					air_ratio = 0        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
					keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
						always = yes
					}
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				SHX = {
					country_event = shx.20
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character = PLM_zhu_shifu
						}
						PLM_zhu_shifu = {
							set_nationality = SHX
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_character = PLM_bai_haifeng
						}
						PLM_bai_haifeng = {
							set_nationality = SHX
						}
					}
					transfer_units_fraction = {
						target = SHX         # the recipient			                      
						size = 0 
						army_ratio = 0.01      # Overrides size modifier for army
						stockpile_ratio = 0  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
						navy_ratio = 0       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
						air_ratio = 0        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
							always = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Gao gave up land and leave for suiyuan
	id = shc.6
	title = shc.6.t
	desc = shc.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_yulin_city
	fire_only_once = yes
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = SHC
		1016 = {
		    is_owned_and_controlled_by = SHC
		}
		has_war_together_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
		OR = {
			621 = {
				owner = {
					#controls_state = 621
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = JAP
					}					
				}
			}
			615 = {
				owner = {
					#controls_state = 621
					has_war_together_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						is_ally_with = JAP
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			is_neighbor_of = event_target:WTT_communist_china
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					621 = {
						owner = {
							#controls_state = 621
							has_war_together_with = ROOT
							NOT = {
								is_ally_with = JAP
							}
							has_war_together_with = event_target:WTT_communist_china
						}
					}
				}
				621 = {
					owner = {
						save_global_event_target_as = suiyuan_owner
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				615 = {
					owner = {
						save_global_event_target_as = suiyuan_owner
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 6
	}
	option = {
		name = shc.6.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		#event_target:suiyuan_owner 
		event_target:WTT_current_china_leader = {
			country_event = shc.7
		}
		event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
			country_event = shc.8
		}
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			#target = event_target:suiyuan_owner '
			target = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader     # the recipient
			size = 0.1    
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
				always = yes
			}
		}
		#SHC_gao_shuangcheng = {
		#	hidden_effect = {
        #        remove_country_leader_role = {
		#			ideology = despotism
		#		}
		#		remove_country_leader_role = {
		#			ideology = fascism_ideology
		#		}
		#		remove_country_leader_role = {
		#			ideology = conservatism
		#		}
		#		remove_country_leader_role = {
		#			ideology = n_socialism_ideology
		#		}
		#		remove_country_leader_role = {
		#			ideology = marxism
		#		}
		#	}	
		#	set_nationality = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		#}
		SHC_gao_guizhi = {
			set_nationality = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		}

country_event = {
	id = tng.1
	title = tng.1.t
	desc = tng.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_Ma_zhongying
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = tng.1.a
		#yes we want him back
		custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_accept_green
		effect_tooltip = {
		    retire_country_leader = yes
		    #create_country_leader = {
			#	name = TNG_ma_zhongying
			#	desc = "POLITICS_Ma_Zhongying_DESC"
			#	picture = "gfx/leaders/TNG/Portrait_Ma_Zhongying.dds"
			#	expire = "1960.7.22"
			#	ideology = despotism
			#	traits = {
			#		
			#	}
			#}
			TNG_ma_zhongying = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = despotism
						traits = {
						}
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}   
			} 
		    #unlock_national_focus = SIK_ma_return
			add_opinion_modifier = {
	            target = ROOT
	            modifier = tng_accept_our_request
            }
		    custom_effect_tooltip = if_they_refuse_red
			add_opinion_modifier = {
	            target = ROOT
	            modifier = hostile_status
            }
		} 
	    SOV = { 
		    country_event = { id = tng.2 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tng.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = TNG_befriend_soviet
			}
		}
		#ma hushan stay
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Ma hushan flees
	id = tng.8
	title = tng.8.t
	desc = tng.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_36th_division_officers

	is_triggered_only = no
	trigger = {
		tag = TNG
		has_government = neutrality
		has_war_with = SIK
		OR = {
            AND = {
				is_ally_with = KHR
				SIK = { 
					has_volunteers_amount_from = {
						tag = SOV
						count > 0
					}
					has_full_control_of_state = 617
					controls_state = 619
					controls_state = 990
				}
			}
			SIK = { 
				has_volunteers_amount_from = {
					tag = SOV
					count > 0
				}
				has_full_control_of_state = 617
				controls_state = 759
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.7
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tng.8.a
		retire_character = TNG_ma_hushan
		retire_character = TNG_bai_zili

		        name = TNG_n36d_officers
			    desc = "POLITICS_N36_DESC"
			    picture = "gfx/leaders/TNG/Portrait_N36D_Officers.dds"
			    expire = "1965.1.1"
			    ideology = fascism_ideology
			    traits = { }

			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 300
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_government = communism
						has_government = n_socialism
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		random_neighbor_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SIK
			    has_government = communism
			    NOT = {
				    is_subject = yes
				    is_ally_with = ROOT
				    has_war_with = PRC
			    }
			}    
		    country_event = {
				id = tng.29 hours = 24
		    }
		}	
		custom_effect_tooltip = sik_and_west_route_army_may_attack_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #trade with xsm
	id = tng_trade.1
	title = tng_trade.1.t	
	desc = tng_trade.1.desc
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_cavalry
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = tng_trade.1.a
		#get 3k ammo with 200 guns
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				has_political_power > 200
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		custom_effect_tooltip = receive_3k_ammo
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 200
			producer = XSM
		}
		add_to_variable = { TNG.ammunition_variable = 3 }
		XSM = {
			country_event = tng_trade.2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = TNG_XSM_trade
				}
			}
		    activate_mission = TNG_XSM_trade
		}
		set_global_flag = tng_trade_xsm_1_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = tng_trade.1.b
		#get 1k ammo with 70 guns
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				has_political_power > 100
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
        custom_effect_tooltip = receive_1k_ammo
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 70
			producer = XSM
		}
		add_to_variable = { TNG.ammunition_variable = 1 }
		XSM = {
			country_event = tng_trade.2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = TNG_XSM_trade
				}
			}
		    activate_mission = TNG_XSM_trade
		}
		set_global_flag = tng_trade_xsm_2_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = tng_trade.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		#not interested!
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_active_mission = TNG_XSM_trade
				}
			}
		    activate_mission = TNG_XSM_trade
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tng_trade.1.d
		#stop trading
		custom_effect_tooltip = trading_will_be_disabled_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #establish advance army? to the roc (if exist) or SUY
	id = suy.1
	title = suy.1.t
	desc = {
		text = suy.1.d_chi
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = SUY
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = suy.1.d_suy
		trigger = {
			tag = SUY
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_ma_zhanshan
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = suy.1.a
		#yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				}
				tag = SUY
			}
			add_corps_commander_role = {
				character = SUY_ma_zhanshan
				traits = { NRA_Lieut_General cavalry_officer war_hero }
				skill=3
				attack_skill=2
				defense_skill=3
				planning_skill=3
				logistics_skill=2
				legacy_id=-1
			}
			SUY_ma_zhanshan = {
				add_advisor_role = {
					activate = yes
					advisor = {
						slot = high_command
						ledger = army
						cost = 100
						idea_token = SUY_ma_zhanshan
						traits = {
							army_cavalry_2
						}
					}
				}
			}	
			custom_effect_tooltip = recruit_ne_advance_army_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = northeastern_advance_army
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				NOT = {
					tag = SUY
				}
			}
		    custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		    add_war_support = 0.025
			#custom_effect_tooltip = send_1_divsion_to_suiyuan_tt
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = suy.2 hours = 12
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					add_corps_commander_role = {
						character = SUY_ma_zhanshan
						traits = { NRA_Lieut_General cavalry_officer war_hero }
						skill=3
						attack_skill=2
						defense_skill=3
						planning_skill=3
						logistics_skill=2
						legacy_id=-1
					}
					SUY_ma_zhanshan = {
						add_advisor_role = {
							activate = yes
							advisor = {
								slot = high_command
								ledger = army
								cost = 100
								idea_token = SUY_ma_zhanshan
								traits = {
									army_cavalry_2
								}
							}
						}
					}	
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = recruit_ne_advance_army_tt
		    }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
				tag = SUY
			}
			add_corps_commander_role = {
				character = SUY_ma_zhanshan
				traits = { NRA_Lieut_General cavalry_officer war_hero }
				skill=3
				attack_skill=2
				defense_skill=3
				planning_skill=3
				logistics_skill=2
				legacy_id=-1
			}
			SUY_ma_zhanshan = {
				add_advisor_role = {
					activate = yes
					advisor = {
						slot = high_command
						ledger = army
						cost = 100
						idea_token = SUY_ma_zhanshan
						traits = {
							army_cavalry_2
						}
					}
				}
			}	
			custom_effect_tooltip = recruit_ne_advance_army_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = northeastern_advance_army
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = suy.1.b
		#refuse
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = SUY
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_war_support = -0.1
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = EFM_independent.51 hours = 12 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #ikechao incident
	id = suy.3
	title = suy.3.t
	desc = suy.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SOV_mongolia_cavalry
	#fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = suy.3.a
		#crack down mongolians
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = THIS_IS_HISTORICAL_TT
		if = {
			limit = {
				746 = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = chi_mon_autonomy }
				}
			}
			746 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = chi_mon_autonomy_flag
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_mon_autonomy_flag
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = chi_mon_autonomy }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = communism
					}
					any_neighbor_country = {
						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = may_trigger_mongolian_rebellion_tt
				event_target:WTT_communist_china = {
					country_event = {
						id = suy.4 days = 3
					}
				}
			    else = {
					add_war_support = -0.1
					add_political_power = -100
					746 = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						add_building_construction = {
							type = industrial_complex
							level = 1
							instant_build = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}	
        if = {
			limit = {
				746 = { 
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = chi_mon_autonomy_weak }
				}
			}
			746 = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = chi_mon_autonomy_weak }
			}
			add_war_support = -0.08
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = suy.3.b
		#give up
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_political_power = -25
	}
}

			        } 
			    }

                        state = 621

						state = 1014

					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			} 
			diplomatic_relation = {
                country = FROM
                relation = non_aggression_pact
            }
		} 
	}

		}

		}
	}

#Sichuan Clique SIC
add_namespace = sic
#Deng Xihou becomes leader
country_event = {
	id = sic.1
	title = sic.1.t
	desc = sic.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = no
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
		tag = SIC
	    has_country_leader = {
			character = SIC_Deng_Xihou ruling_only = yes
		}
		is_subject_of = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
		has_autonomy_state = autonomy_rcm_national_revolutionary_army	
	}
	option = {
		name = sic.1.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SIC
			}
			overlord = {
				country_event = {
					id = sic.1 hours = 12
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_rcm_provincial_government
				}		
			}
			add_political_power = 100
			add_stability = 0.05
			else = {
				effect_tooltip = {
					SIC = {
						overlord = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = ROOT
								autonomy_state = autonomy_rcm_provincial_government
							}
						}
						add_political_power = 100
						add_stability = 0.05
					}
				}
				add_stability = 0.03
			}
		}	
	}
}

country_event = { #SIC rebellion to xik and yun
	id = sic.5
	title = sic.5.t
	desc = sic.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = sic.5.a
		#join
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_enemy_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_ally_with = JAP
				}
			}
			white_peace = ROOT
		}
		FROM = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = {
				id = sic.9 hours = 24
			} 
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = sic.5.b
		#refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = EFM_independent.51 hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = sic.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
                remove_ideas = CHI_zhang_qun_in_sic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = zhang_qun
			}
			retire_character = zhang_qun
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				white_peace = JAP
				#set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
				create_faction = "southwest_rebel_faction"
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}

	option = {
		name = sic.6.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
                remove_ideas = CHI_zhang_qun_in_sic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = zhang_qun
			}

				set_autonomy = {
					target = ROOT
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				white_peace = JAP

		}

			target = SIC
		}
	}

country_event = { #SIC generals join CHI to SIC
	id = sic.7
	title = sic.7.t
	desc = sic.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = sic.7.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SIC_liu_xiang ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					owns_state = 1041
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 1041
					}
				}
			    1041 = {
					set_state_owner_to = FROM
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 751
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 751
					}
				}
			    751 = {
					set_state_owner_to = FROM
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SIC_liu_xiang ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
					1041 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				1041 = {
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					751 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				751 = {
					transfer_state_to = FROM
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = SIC_liu_xiang ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_character = SIC_Wang_Lingji
							#is_character = SIC_Wang_Zuanxu
							is_character = SIC_Yang_Sen
							is_character = SIC_Tang_Shizun
							is_character = SIC_Sun_Zhen
							is_character = SIC_Li_Jiayu
						}
					}
					set_nationality = FROM
				}
				else = {
					every_unit_leader = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								#is_character = SIC_Wang_Lingji
								#is_character = SIC_Wang_Zuanxu
								is_character = SIC_Yang_Sen
								#is_character = SIC_Tang_Shizun
								is_character = SIC_Sun_Zhen
								is_character = SIC_Li_Jiayu
							}
						}
						set_nationality = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			transfer_units_fraction = {
			    target = FROM   # the recipient			                      
			    size = 0 
				army_ratio = 0.5      # Overrides size modifier for army
			    stockpile_ratio = 0  # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for the stockpiled equipment and fuel
			    navy_ratio = 0       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy
			    air_ratio = 0        # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for air
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { # Trigger for unit leaders to remain with the original country
				    always = yes
			    }
		    }
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = sic.8 hours = 12
			}
		}
	}
}

			    navy_ratio = 0       # [0,1] Overrides size modifier for navy

				}
			    every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 1041
							#state = 1023
							state = 605
							state = 751
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Li Jishen Dismissed (inviter hidden)
	id = rcm_warlord_invite_li_jishen.3
	#fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	#mean_time_to_happen = {
	#	days = 8
	#}
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = li_jishen_invited_country
		save_event_target_as = previous_inviter
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.literally_china_including_chinese_puppets
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { is_originally_warlord = yes tag = PLM } NOT = { tag = ROOT } }
				country_event = rcm_warlord_invite_li_jishen.4
			}
		}
		clr_global_flag = li_jishen_invited
	}
	option = {
	}
}
